Product support included

What's Product Support?

In the event your product doesn't work as expected or you need help using it, Amazon offers free product support options such as live phone/chat with an Amazon associate, manufacturer contact information, step-by-step troubleshooting guides, and help videos.
By solving product issues, we help the planet by extending the life of products. Availability of support options differ by product and country.  [Learn more](/ps/product-support?ref_=dp_pls_support&ref_=dp_ret_policy)

How trade-in works

How trade-in works

![Upgrade and save](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/G/01/tradein/WIP/how_delivery.png)

1. Upgrade and save

Accept your estimated trade-in value, buy your new device at the current price, and receive your delivery.

![Prepare device](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/G/01/tradein/WIP/how_tell_us.png)

2. Prepare device

Sign out of all accounts linked to your old device, and factory reset it to erase your personal information.

![Ship within 30 days](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/G/01/tradein/WIP/how_send.png)

3. Ship within 30 days

Print your shipping label, [package your old device](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html?ref_=hp_left_v4_sib&nodeId=G2Q9VNXJ29E7AK89), and drop it off at any UPS location within 30 days of receiving your new device.

![Get your rebate](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/G/01/tradein/WIP/2_how_rebate.png)

4. Get your rebate

After we receive your trade-in device, we'll verify it within 10 business days. Once verified, you'll receive your [trade-in value](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html?ref_=hp_left_v4_sib&nodeId=GNESDAAB2JL84N3A) as an Amazon.com Gift Card to your Amazon account for immediate use.

# About this item

* ACTIVATION REQUIRED: After purchase, users will select a monthly data plan. Starter plan: $29/mo. Wi-Fi only: $39/mo. 4GB: $49/mo. 8GB: $59/mo. UNLIMITED GB: $79/mo.
* STATE-OF-THE-ART MONITORING: Get alerts for potential issues in your child’s texts, emails and 30+ social media platforms and apps. Scan for online predators, sexting, suicidal ideation, bullying, violence, drugs/alcohol, and more.
* APPROVE APPS AND CONTACTS: Manage the apps your child can install as well as who they can text and call.
* TAMPER-PROOF PARENTAL CONTROLS: The rules you set stay in place. Plus, texts can't be deleted without your permission.
* REAL-TIME GPS LOCATION TRACKING: We make location sharing simple with three different ways to keep track of your child — a real-time map, customizable location alerts, and check-ins.

# hero-video

 Merchant Video

* ### What type of phone is it?

  The Bark Phone is a Samsung A16. We designed it so that it wouldn’t be recognizable as a kid’s phone — Bark’s parental controls are all internal. Whether you have an iPhone or an Android, you will be able to manage the Bark Phone with no issues.
* ### How much do Bark Phone plans cost?

  Our monthly subscription plans range from $29 to $79 per month. Plans include the device, built-in parental controls, unlimited talk & text, data (if you need it), and a Bark Premium subscription. Choose the plan that fits your family’s needs.
* ### What does the Bark Phone come with?

  Every Bark Phone comes with: Unlimited talk and text, Bark Premium subscription for the entire family, USB-C charging cord, a data plan that fits your family’s needs (non-starter plans only), and a quick start guide for easy setup
* ### What apps are available for the Bark Phone?

  We have two options: the starter plan is our locked-down version perfect for younger kids or teens who need more supervision. It allows for texting and calling only; our advanced plans allow your child to request any apps in the Google Play store.
* ### How is the Bark Phone different from other kids' phones?

  The Bark Phone offers advanced content monitoring, scanning texts, photos, videos, apps, and social media for dangers, alerting you if needed. It’s customizable, with a starter plan for younger kids and an upgradeable advanced plan as they grow.

How customer reviews and ratings work

Customer Reviews, including Product Star Ratings help customers to learn more about the product and decide whether it is the right product for them.

To calculate the overall star rating and percentage breakdown by star, we don’t use a simple average. Instead, our system considers things like how recent a review is and if the reviewer bought the item on Amazon. It also analyzed reviews to verify trustworthiness.

[Learn more how customers reviews work on Amazon](/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref%3Dcm_cr_dp_d_omni_lm_btn?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)

### Customers say

Customers find this phone suitable for young children, particularly pre-teens, and appreciate its ease of use, especially for 9-year-olds. The device offers comprehensive safety features, including real-time 24/7 GPS tracking and customizable parental controls that provide a good balance between freedom and supervision. Customers like the alerts system, which sends notifications for concerning activities, and one customer notes the GPS tracking is very accurate. The functionality receives mixed reviews, with some saying it works great while others report issues with apps not working properly.

  ##### [*5.0 out of 5 stars* Tired of Apple screen time failing get the bark phone.](/gp/customer-reviews/REIHRQ05C9899/ref%3Dcm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8)

  Reviewed in the United States on December 29, 2025

  Color: Black-Pro[Verified Purchase](/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref%3Dcm_cr_dp_d_rvw_avp?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)

  I really wish I would’ve switched my daughter to the Bark Phone long ago. If you are debating between a standard smartphone with a parental control app versus this dedicated phone, go with the Bark Phone.
  Here is why it’s a game-changer for our family:
  • Truly Tamper-Proof: Unlike standard phones where kids can find "workarounds," this has much tighter lockdowns. One of my favorite features is that the dashboard alerts me immediately if she tries to turn the phone off or switch it to Airplane Mode to "go dark."
  • Safety Without Being Invasive: It strikes the perfect balance for us. I can track her location via GPS, but I don’t have to spend hours scrolling through every single one of her texts. Bark’s AI only notifies me when it detects something concerning (like bullying or risky content), which builds trust while keeping her safe.
  • Works Across All Devices: I love that the Bark subscription included with the phone also works across her other devices (tablets, computers, etc.). Managing everything from one central dashboard is a huge time-saver.
  • Customizable Growth: It’s not just a "little kid" phone. You can start with zero apps and slowly "unlock" features like the browser or social media as they get older and show more responsibility.
  Bottom Line: If you're tired of "policing" a regular iPhone or Android, this is worth every penny. It takes the stress out of digital parenting and lets you be a parent rather than a private investigator.

  Read more

  Jill P](/gp/profile/amzn1.account.AFFBFQH3ZTPRQUFCEBA3ZWYVEEHQ)

  ##### [*4.0 out of 5 stars* Almost perfect](/gp/customer-reviews/R1CBVUKWLV3B60/ref%3Dcm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8)

  Reviewed in the United States on June 24, 2025

  Color: Black-A16[Verified Purchase](/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref%3Dcm_cr_dp_d_rvw_avp?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)

  We were looking for a first cell phone for our 11 year old and wanted one that looked like regular phones, but had a strong monitoring aspect. After months of research, we decided to go with a bark phone and couldn't be happier. The phone is the same Samsung A16 my husband and I have, so we know it's a great device. The real gem here is the Bark phone plan with monitoring. We chose to go with the lowest tier plan, which includes unlimited talk and text but no internet access. Talk and text is all we wanted for our child at this point. The plan also includes location monitoring and my child can take and send photos.

  We have the ability to upgrade the plan at any time, which is wonderful. I also love that in the future, when my child is much older, the Bark phone number can be transferred to another phone plan so my child can still keep their phone number. We had the option to buy the phone through the Bark website and pay for it monthly in addition to our phone plan, but chose to buy it outright from Bark through Amazon, which was what we had planned on doing. The phone was less than $250, which is incredible for a quality, name brand phone. Setting up the phone was extremely easy using the instructions included from Bark. The Parent app is great and I love that I get notifications on my phone and that I can update sensitivity settings, contacts, location services, etc on my phone.

  My one complaint that stopped me from giving a five star review is that my child was not supposed to receive calls or texts from unknown contacts, as the Bark programing only allows contact with approved contacts. This may have been a glitch, but for the first few days with the phone, we would get calls come through (we never answered them) from a local utility company, as well as texts alerting for automatic bill pay with a road toll company, electric company, etc. My understanding was that these were not supposed to come through as they were not listed as approved contacts. I blocked each text that came as well as the calls and made sure that I added the Bark ohine number to the No Call Registry, and we had no issues after the first 4 days. Again, may have been a glitch or maybe automated texts that come from five or six digit numbers aren't blocked, not certain.

  Overall, I would recommend this phone and the Bark phone service to anyone. I see us upgrading the phone plan in the future to allow for app and internet use, but it's not needed right now. We also plan to buy a second Bark phone in a few years for our second child when they are ready for a phone.

  Read more

  67 people found this helpful

Product support included

What's Product Support?

In the event your product doesn't work as expected or you need help using it, Amazon offers free product support options such as live phone/chat with an Amazon associate, manufacturer contact information, step-by-step troubleshooting guides, and help videos.
By solving product issues, we help the planet by extending the life of products. Availability of support options differ by product and country.  [Learn more](/ps/product-support?ref_=dp_pls_support&ref_=dp_ret_policy)

Get your estimated trade-in value

How trade-in works

How trade-in works

![Upgrade and save](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/G/01/tradein/WIP/how_delivery.png)

1. Upgrade and save

Accept your estimated trade-in value, buy your new device at the current price, and receive your delivery.

![Prepare device](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/G/01/tradein/WIP/how_tell_us.png)

2. Prepare device

Sign out of all accounts linked to your old device, and factory reset it to erase your personal information.

![Ship within 30 days](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/G/01/tradein/WIP/how_send.png)

3. Ship within 30 days

Print your shipping label, [package your old device](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html?ref_=hp_left_v4_sib&nodeId=G2Q9VNXJ29E7AK89), and drop it off at any UPS location within 30 days of receiving your new device.

![Get your rebate](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/G/01/tradein/WIP/2_how_rebate.png)

4. Get your rebate

After we receive your trade-in device, we'll verify it within 10 business days. Once verified, you'll receive your [trade-in value](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html?ref_=hp_left_v4_sib&nodeId=GNESDAAB2JL84N3A) as an Amazon.com Gift Card to your Amazon account for immediate use.

## What is Amazon Renewed?

Amazon Renewed is your trusted destination for products that are inspected, tested, and refurbished as necessary to be fully functional.

![](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/11X1grO0K6L.png)

#### Quality you can afford

Amazon Renewed products offer an affordable option so you can save on the brands you love.

![](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/11m5NyTwLVL.png)

#### Products you can trust

All products have been professionally inspected, tested, cleaned, and refurbished as necessary by Amazon-qualified suppliers. Products are not certified by Apple.

![](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/11MpO5lMksL.png)

#### Purchases with an impact

Your Amazon Renewed purchase extends the lifetime of this product and reduces electronic waste.

![](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/118nlf+F3RL.png)

#### Trusted coverage

Your purchase is eligible for Amazon Renewed coverage in conjunction with Amazon's Return Policy and the A-to-z Guarantee.

#### What should I expect to receive with my Amazon Renewed purchase?

All Amazon Renewed purchases will come with accessories equivalent to those that shipped in the box when new. These items may not be original but will be compatible and fully functional. Amazon Renewed products will be packaged in either original packaging or in a new and clean cardboard box.

#### Model Year

2023

#### In what condition can I expect my Amazon Renewed product to be?

Product will be restored to its original factory settings and will be in one of the following cosmetic conditions Premium, Excellent, Good or Acceptable. [Learn more](/gp/help/customer/display.html?nodeId=202089470)

Shop for smartphones, computers, laptops, tablets, home and kitchen appliances, game consoles, office products, and more. [Visit Amazon Renewed](/renewed)

How customer reviews and ratings work

Customer Reviews, including Product Star Ratings help customers to learn more about the product and decide whether it is the right product for them.

To calculate the overall star rating and percentage breakdown by star, we don’t use a simple average. Instead, our system considers things like how recent a review is and if the reviewer bought the item on Amazon. It also analyzed reviews to verify trustworthiness.

[Learn more how customers reviews work on Amazon](/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref%3Dcm_cr_dp_d_omni_lm_btn?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)

### Customers say

Customers find the iPhone to be in perfect condition, like new, with a 100% battery life and good value for money. They appreciate its appearance, noting it looks like new with brand new screen and case, and one customer mentions the speakers work great. The phone's functionality receives mixed feedback, with some reporting it works like new while others say it doesn't work properly. Similarly, the unlock status is mixed, with some customers confirming it's unlocked while others report it being locked. The scratch resistance also gets mixed reviews, with some customers reporting no scratches while others mention scratches on the screen.

##### Definitely worth upgrading (Premium Unlocked)

So far so good. Transferring esim is easier than I thought. I got the premium unlocked and the maximum capacity is not bad. Camera quality is amazing compared to my 4 years old phone. It feels nice and new. No scratches, dent, or discoloration. It looks durable. And the green color is amazing in person. Definitely worth it if you're under budget. I would highly get the premium one.

Get your estimated trade-in value

How trade-in works

How trade-in works

![Upgrade and save](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/G/01/tradein/WIP/how_delivery.png)

1. Upgrade and save

Accept your estimated trade-in value, buy your new device at the current price, and receive your delivery.

![Prepare device](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/G/01/tradein/WIP/how_tell_us.png)

2. Prepare device

Sign out of all accounts linked to your old device, and factory reset it to erase your personal information.

![Ship within 30 days](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/G/01/tradein/WIP/how_send.png)

3. Ship within 30 days

Print your shipping label, [package your old device](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html?ref_=hp_left_v4_sib&nodeId=G2Q9VNXJ29E7AK89), and drop it off at any UPS location within 30 days of receiving your new device.

![Get your rebate](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/G/01/tradein/WIP/2_how_rebate.png)

4. Get your rebate

After we receive your trade-in device, we'll verify it within 10 business days. Once verified, you'll receive your [trade-in value](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html?ref_=hp_left_v4_sib&nodeId=GNESDAAB2JL84N3A) as an Amazon.com Gift Card to your Amazon account for immediate use.

# About this item

* Premium Performance: Powered by the latest A18 Pro chip for ultra-fast performance, advanced AI features, seamless multitasking, and smooth gaming.
* Stunning 6.9" ProMotion Display: Super Retina XDR OLED display with adaptive 120Hz refresh rate for incredibly smooth scrolling and vibrant visuals.
* Pro-Level Camera System: Advanced 48MP main camera with enhanced zoom, Night mode, macro photography, and 4K Dolby Vision video recording.
* 256GB Storage Capacity: Ample space for high-resolution photos, 4K videos, apps, and files.
* Unlocked US Version: Compatible with major U.S. carriers and global networks (eSIM supported).
* Durable Black Titanium Design: Lightweight yet strong titanium frame with Ceramic Shield front for enhanced durability.
* All-Day Battery Life: Long-lasting battery with fast charging, USB-C connectivity, and MagSafe/Qi wireless charging support.
* Renewed Premium Condition: Professionally inspected, tested, and cleaned to work like new, delivering flagship performance at exceptional value from Apple Inc..

## What is Amazon Renewed?

Amazon Renewed is your trusted destination for products that are inspected, tested, and refurbished as necessary to be fully functional.

![](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/11X1grO0K6L.png)

#### Quality you can afford

Amazon Renewed products offer an affordable option so you can save on the brands you love.

![](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/11m5NyTwLVL.png)

#### Products you can trust

All products have been professionally inspected, tested, cleaned, and refurbished as necessary by Amazon-qualified suppliers. Products are not certified by Apple.

![](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/11MpO5lMksL.png)

#### Purchases with an impact

Your Amazon Renewed purchase extends the lifetime of this product and reduces electronic waste.

![](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/118nlf+F3RL.png)

#### Trusted coverage

Your purchase is eligible for Amazon Renewed coverage in conjunction with Amazon's Return Policy and the A-to-z Guarantee.

#### What should I expect to receive with my Amazon Renewed purchase?

All Amazon Renewed purchases will come with accessories equivalent to those that shipped in the box when new. These items may not be original but will be compatible and fully functional. Amazon Renewed products will be packaged in either original packaging or in a new and clean cardboard box.

#### Model Year

2024

#### In what condition can I expect my Amazon Renewed product to be?

Product will be restored to its original factory settings and will be in one of the following cosmetic conditions Premium, Excellent, Good or Acceptable. [Learn more](/gp/help/customer/display.html?nodeId=202089470)

Shop for smartphones, computers, laptops, tablets, home and kitchen appliances, game consoles, office products, and more. [Visit Amazon Renewed](/renewed)

How customer reviews and ratings work

Customer Reviews, including Product Star Ratings help customers to learn more about the product and decide whether it is the right product for them.

To calculate the overall star rating and percentage breakdown by star, we don’t use a simple average. Instead, our system considers things like how recent a review is and if the reviewer bought the item on Amazon. It also analyzed reviews to verify trustworthiness.

[Learn more how customers reviews work on Amazon](/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref%3Dcm_cr_dp_d_omni_lm_btn?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)

### Customers say

Customers find this iPhone to be in excellent condition, with 99% battery health and no scratches reported. The phone functions well and is easy to set up, with one customer noting it works through E-sim. They appreciate its appearance and consider it worth the price, with one mentioning it comes with 99% battery life. The scratch resistance receives mixed feedback - while some report no scratches, others mention receiving phones with scratches.

Amazon Customer

*5 out of 5 stars*

##### iPhone 16 pro max upgrade!!! <3 so happy

Honestly, I’m really happy I decided to make this purchase for myself. I got the Apple iPhone 16 Pro Max because I needed an upgrade but didn’t want to completely break the bank. The phone arrived exactly as described & in almost mint condition — no scratches on the screen or body at all (I got the renewed premium) & battery health was at 91%! The camera quality is amazing & definitely a noticeable upgrade from my previous phone. The connectivity has been great so far with fast service & Wi-Fi, & everything runs really smoothly. The phone unlock feature works perfectly & is super quick, which makes it really convenient to use throughout the day. I also love the larger screen size since I watch a lot of content on my phone — it makes videos & apps look so much better. It uses a USB-C charger which was included with the phone purchase (I was not expecting) , which is new for me, but I actually like it because it charges quickly & feels more modern. The phone itself feels very durable & well made. Overall, I’m really happy with the upgrade and glad I decided to go with this phone.

  ##### Basically brand new!! No flaws I'm super happy!

  Reviewed in the United States on March 3, 2026

  My mom wanted a bigger phone, so i figured I'd upgrade to a 16 Pro Max and give my mom my 14 Pro Max. Saw the renewed ones on Amazon and thought I'd give it a shot. I'm glad I did! ZERO scratches or cosmetic damage. Looked brand new. Size is the same to my 14 PM. SOOOO easy to switch my data and phone number over. Quality is excellent. Checked out the battery life: still at 98% health for the battery! Best of all, it still has Apple care til Oct 2026 so I have tons of time in case anything funky happens. I haven't noticed any kind of lag at all, but I am genuinely impressed with how pristine this renewed iPhone is! Very happy I got it! it's working perfectly and my mom is happy with my 14 PM, so it really was worth it 10 out of 10! I also feel safer knowing that I have the Premium warranty on it through Amazon. This was a great purchase!

  LoveMeSomeAmazon](/gp/profile/amzn1.account.AGZG7M3NOTCTAJAOK45CRHJ7V3VQ)

  ##### [*5.0 out of 5 stars* Great Phone - Not so happy with the trade-in process](/gp/customer-reviews/R2IHFUCCBQW9LF/ref%3Dcm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8)

  Reviewed in the United States on January 10, 2026

  Size: 256GBColor: Desert TitaniumService provider: T-MobileProduct grade: Renewed Premium[Verified Purchase](/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref%3Dcm_cr_dp_d_rvw_avp?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)

  I needed a new phone because I was fed up with my 15 that I'd gone el cheapo on. It was too small compared to the android I had switched from, and it didn't have enough storage space so it was to the point that I didn't even have space to install updates and that caused some weird things like my calendar events just disappearing.

  I'm not great at texting with my thumbs. My vision isn't what it used to be, I guess the pads of my thumbs aren't as full either. I struggled with texting so I tended to use the voice-to-text feature mostly. And even though they've been doing dictation software since the 90s, it's still pretty terrible. Don't get me started on the camera either. My android's camera blew the iPhone's out of the water and it was at least 3 years older.

  So, this 16 Pro Max phone hits on a few areas that I was looking to improve and it does it well. It's the largest screen they offer and comes with twice the storage. The voice-to-text seems to be somewhat better but still causes some frustration at times. The camera is much better but I'm still not sure if it's better than the old android.

  But now I have to talk about the fact that this is a "renewed" phone to begin with. I went with the "Renewed Premium" because I wanted as close to a new phone as possible but without spending all that money. I considered this the last chance I would give to Apple before I switched back to Android - I didn't want to pay a fortune to find out that I was still unsatisfied - and this seemed the best route to take.

  I was not disappointed. Other than not coming in an iPhone box, there wasn't the slightest clue that it was not a new phone, cosmetically. I had no issues getting it set up - I mean it was crazy easy using the tools / instructions that you can find just by going into AI mode on a Google search. I love my phone now. My old mantra was "I hate this phone" or "This phone is a piece of ..." . I had dreams of running it over with my car.

  I haven't had any issue with the functionality of this renewed phone either. I'm finding a lot of features that are endearing me to the brand too. I don't have to worry about storage, I have a larger screen (but I'm still not that much better at texting), and I'm dealing with the voice to text still. But as far as the product I received, I'm soooo very happy I went this route.

  Now for the thing that I really was disappointed about. The trade-in value of my old phone (which was in excellent condition) is about $35 less than I would have gotten through Apple - but they only sell the most current version of a Pro Max phone, so I couldn't have gotten the 16 Pro Max through them anyway as the 17 model was already out in stores.

  When I was working with my budget I thought that the $275 would be taken off the price of the phone but I can see now how naive it was to think that. They're not going to give you money for a phone upfront, sight unseen. So I just figured that it would work out since they would apply the credit back to the card once they'd received and checked out my trade-in.

  Ooooh was I mistaken! First of all, they do not treat it like a refund where they add the funds to your original method of payment. Instead, you get Amazon credit. And by credit, I mean that you can ONLY spend that money on Amazon.

  You cannot buy a gift card offered on Amazon for another store (for example, Best Buy), you cannot even get an Amazon gift card with it. I needed the funds to go towards my car stereo that I was planning to buy at a different store (because they install it for free as long as I purchase it from them) but I wasn't permitted to use the credit on that. I thought that maybe I could get it in a Amazon gift card, and then get my friend to buy that from me. Nope.

  If it weren't for the trade in process I would have been 100% happy with my purchase.

  It's only because this phone was exactly as described and pictured that I am happy. And ultimately, things worked out for me with the trade-in credit situation when my son was buying an eScooter and agreed to send me the money so I could purchase it from my account and apply that credit towards the purchase.

  So the moral of the story is that this renewed phone was a great route to go (I'm speaking to the Renewed Premium offerings), and I was very happy with the phone, both cosmetically and functionally. You just need to be fully aware of how the trade-in works (and its limitations) so you don't get frustrated in the end.

  Read more

  Reviewed in the United States on December 5, 2025

  Size: 256GBColor: Black TitaniumService provider: UnlockedProduct grade: Renewed[Verified Purchase](/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref%3Dcm_cr_dp_d_rvw_avp?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)

  I bought the Apple iPhone 16 Pro Max (US Version, 256GB, Black Titanium) in renewed condition, and overall I’m very satisfied. The phone does have some noticeable scratches on the upper and lower sides of the body, which is why I’m giving it 4 stars instead of 5. However, the display itself is in excellent condition with no issues.

  Once the phone is in a case, the scratches aren’t visible, and everything else works perfectly. Performance is fast and smooth, and the battery health is at 100%, which is impressive for a renewed device. Being fully unlocked is another big plus.

  A solid value overall — just expect some cosmetic wear.
